posted:Posted March 24, 2024
msg:The basic hardware facilities meet the standards of a five-star hotel.
1. The hotel is located in the High-tech Zone, close to the destination company for business trips, with convenient transportation. It takes only ten minutes to drive to Weifang North High-speed Railway Station.
2. The hotel is relatively quiet, but there are relatively few catering, entertainment and other supporting facilities around it.
3. The hotel rooms are spacious, and the electric curtains will open when you enter the room, showing a wide view.
4. The room layout is relatively good and the facilities are relatively new. Hisense's Internet TV is equipped with Shandong HDTV system. The bathroom is equipped with a smart toilet.
5. All toiletries are from Shiseido. It's just that the bathing in the room is a bit awkward, with a very small bathtub and no separate shower room. You have to stand in the bathtub when taking a bath.
6. The breakfast variety is rich, but the breakfast on Saturday morning ended at 9:30. I have stayed in many five-star hotels, and this one is the earliest to end. I went to eat at 9:40 on Saturday, and the restaurant was already cleaning.
7. The hotel service is acceptable. A small gift was given when checking out, and there was also a phone call to track the check-in experience.
Overall, it's okay, and the price-performance ratio is good. If guests often stay in five-star hotels and pursue the ultimate accommodation experience, then the hotel still has a lot of room for improvement.
